## Prompt Set (ps_1773497855498)

**Time:** 2026-03-14T14:17:35.498Z
**Duration:** 0ms
**Tool Calls:** 1

### Text Exchange - 2026-03-14 14:17:35 UTC [15:17:35 CEST]

**Assistant Response:** The fix: also check that a Claude or coding agent process is actually running in the pane, not just that the pane exists with that cwd. The simplest approach: check if the pane has a Claude/copilot/opencode process running (not just a shell), by using `#{pane_current_command}` or checking child processes.

Actually, the cleaner fix is to also check `#{session_name}` and verify the tmux session is a `coding-*` session with a running agent:


**Type:** Text-only exchange (no tool calls)

---

### Edit - 2026-03-14 14:17:35 UTC [15:17:35 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>obal-lsl-coordinator.js",
  "old_string": "  async hasActiveTmuxSession(projectName) {\n    try {\n      // Get pane working directories for all sessions\n      const { stdout } = await execAsync(\n        'tmux list-panes -a -F \"#{pane_current_path}\" 2>/dev/null'\n      );\n      const paths = stdout.trim().split('\\n').filter(Boolean);\n      // Match if any pane is working in this project's directory\n      return paths.some(p => path.basename(p) === projectName || p.endsWith(`/${projectName}`));\n    } catch {\n      return false; // tmux not running or error — assume no session\n    }\n  }",
  "new_string": "  async hasActiveTmuxSession(projectName) {\n    try {\n      // Get pane working directories AND the process running in each pane.\n      // A pane with the right cwd but only a bare shell (no claude/copilot/opencode)\n      // is a stale session that should be pruned.\n      const { stdout } = await execAsync(\n        'tmux list-panes -a -F \"#{pane_current_path}|#{pane_current_command}\" 2>/dev/null'\n      );\n      const lines = stdout.trim().split('\\n').filter(Boolean);\n      return lines.some(line => {\n        const [panePath, paneCmd] = line.split('|');\n        const pathMatches = path.basename(panePath) === projectName || panePath.endsWith(`/${projectName}`);\n        if (!pathMatches) return false;\n        // Check if a coding agent is actually running (not just a bare shell)\n        const agentPatterns = ['claude', 'copilot', 'opencode', 'node', 'python'];\n        const cmd = (paneCmd || '').toLowerCase();\n        return agentPatterns.some(p => cmd.includes(p));\n      });\n    } catch {\n      return false; // tmux not running or error — assume no session\n    }\n  }"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
The file <AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>obal-lsl-coordinator.js has been updated successfully.
```

now\n    const substeps = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid^=\"substep-\"]')).map(el => ({\n        id: el.getAttribute('data-testid'),\n document.querySelectorAll('[class*=\"panel\"], [class*=\"sidebar\"], [class*=\"detail\"]');\n        for (const p of panels) {\n          if (p.textContent?.includes('Sub-step') || p.textContent?.includes('substep') || p.textContent?.includes('Processing')) {\n            return p.textContent?.substring(0, 500);\n          }\n        }\n        // Fallback: get all text from the modal\n        const modal = document.querySelector('[role=\"dialog\"], [class*=\"modal\"]');\n        if (modal) return modal.textContent?.substring(modal.textContent.length - 500);\n        return null;\n      });\n      log('  Right panel text: ' + (rightPanelText?.substring(0, 300) || 'none'));\n    } else {\n      for (const s of substeps) {\n        const icon = s.status === 'completed' ? '✅' : s.status === 'running' ? '🔵' : '⬜';\n        log(`  ${icon} ${s.id}: ${s.status}`);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Check: what does the API return for currentStep now?\n    const apiResp = await page.evaluate(async () => {\n      try {\n        const resp = await fetch('http://localhost:3033/api/ukb/status');\n        const data = await resp.json();\n        const proc = data?.data?.processes?.[0];\n        return {\n          currentStep: proc?.currentStep,\n          pausedAtStep: proc?.pausedAtStep,\n          completedSteps: proc?.completedSteps,\n          stepsCount: proc?.steps?.length,\n          stepNames: proc?.steps?.map(s => `${s.name}:${s.status}`).slice(0, 10)\n        };\n      } catch (e) {\n        return { error: e.message };\n      }\n    });\n\n    log('\\n=== API DATA ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(apiResp, null, 2));\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write('Error: ' + err.message + '\\n');\n    process.exit(1);\n  } finally {\n    await browser.close();\n  }\n})();\n"

### Bash - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "node --version && npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null | head -1",
  "description": "Check Playwright availability"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
v25.8.1
Version 1.58.2
```


---

  "file_path": "/tmp/pw-scripts/debug-wf-graph.js",
  "content": "const { chromium } = require('playwright');\n\n(async () => {\n  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });\n  const context = await browser.newContext({ viewport: { width: 1400, height: 900 } });\n  const page = await context.newPage();\n\n  try {\n    await page.goto('http://localhost:3032', { waitUntil: 'networkidle', timeout: 15000 });\n\n    // Click UKB Workflows to open modal\n    await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');\n    await page.waitForTimeout(3000); // Wait for graph to render\n\n    // Screenshot the modal\n    await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/wf-modal.png', fullPage: false });\n\n    // Get all workflow nodes and their statuses\n    const nodes = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const allNodes = document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid^=\"workflow-node-\"]');\n      const results = [];\n      for (const node of allNodes) {\n        results.push({\n          testId: node.getAttribute('data-testid'),\n          status: node.getAttribute('data-status'),\n          className: node.className,\n          style: node.getAttribute('style'),\n          text: node.textContent?.substring(0, 50)\n        });\n      }\n      return results;\n    });\n\n    console.log('=== WORKFLOW NODES ===');\n    console.log(JSON.stringify(nodes, null, 2));\n\n    // Also check if there are SVG circle/rect elements with color indicators\n    const svgElements = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      // Look for elements with fill colors that might indicate status\n      const circles = document.querySelectorAll('circle, rect, ellipse');\n      const colored = [];\n      for (const el of circles) {\n        const fill = el.getAttribute('fill') || window.getComputedStyle(el).fill;\n        const stroke = el.getAttribute('stroke') || window.getComputedStyle(el).stroke;\n        const parent = el.closest('[data-testid]');\n        if (fill && fill !== 'none' && fill !== '') {\n          colored.push({\n            tag: el.tagName,\n            fill,\n            stroke,\n            parentTestId: parent?.getAttribute('data-testid'),\n            parentClass: parent?.className?.substring?.(0, 80)\n          });\n        }\n      }\n      return colored.slice(0, 30); // First 30\n    });\n\n    console.log('\\n=== SVG COLORED ELEMENTS ===');\n    console.log(JSON.stringify(svgElements, null, 2));\n\n    // Check the workflow progress data being used by the frontend\n    const storeState = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      // Try to access Redux store\n      const root = document.getElementById('root');\n      if (root && root._reactRootContainer) {\n        return 'React root found but cannot access store directly';\n      }\n      // Check for any global workflow state\n      return window.__WORKFLOW_STATE__ || window.__STORE__ || 'No global state found';\n    });\n\n    console.log('\\n=== STORE STATE ===');\n    console.log(JSON.stringify(storeState, null, 2));\n\n    // Check what API data the dashboard fetches for workflow status\n    // Intercept the next API call\n    const apiData = await page.evaluate(async () => {\n      try {\n        const resp = await fetch('/api/ukb/status');\n        return await resp.json();\n      } catch (e) {\n        return { error: e.message };\n      }\n    });\n\n    console.log('\\n=== API /api/ukb/status ===');\n    console.log(JSON.stringify(apiData, null, 2).substring(0, 2000));\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error('Error:', err.message);\n    process.exit(1);\n  } finally {\n    await browser.close();\n  }\n})();\n"
}
```

### Write - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/pw-scripts/debug-wf-graph.js",
  "content": "const { chromium } = require('playwright');\n\n(async () => {\n  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });\n  const context = await browser.newContext({ viewport: { width: 1400, height: 900 } });\n  const page = await context.newPage();\n  const log = (msg) => process.stdout.write(msg + '\\n');\n\n  try {\n    await page.goto('http://localhost:3032', { waitUntil: 'networkidle', timeout: 15000 });\n\n    // Click UKB Workflows to open modal\n    await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');\n    await page.waitForTimeout(3000);\n\n    // Screenshot\n    await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/wf-modal.png', fullPage: false });\n\n    // Get all workflow nodes and their statuses\n    const nodes = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const allNodes = document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid^=\"workflow-node-\"]');\n      return Array.from(allNodes).map(node => ({\n        testId: node.getAttribute('data-testid'),\n        status: node.getAttribute('data-status'),\n        className: node.className?.substring?.(0, 100),\n        text: node.textContent?.substring(0, 50)\n      }));\n    });\n\n    log('=== WORKFLOW NODES ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(nodes, null, 2));\n\n    // Check SVG node colors (fills on circles/rects)\n    const svgColors = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const elements = document.querySelectorAll('circle, rect, ellipse, .workflow-node, [class*=\"node\"]');\n      return Array.from(elements).slice(0, 40).map(el => {\n        const computed = window.getComputedStyle(el);\n        return {\n          tag: el.tagName,\n          fill: el.getAttribute('fill') || computed.fill,\n          bg: computed.backgroundColor,\n          cls: (el.className?.baseVal || el.className || '').substring(0, 80),\n          parentTestId: el.closest('[data-testid]')?.getAttribute('data-testid')\n        };\n      }).filter(e => e.fill !== 'none' || e.bg !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)');\n    });\n\n    log('\\n=== SVG COLORS ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(svgColors, null, 2));\n\n    // Get workflow progress API data\n    const apiData = await page.evaluate(async () => {\n      try {\n        const resp = await fetch('/api/ukb/status');\n        return await resp.json();\n      } catch (e) {\n        return { error: e.message };\n      }\n    });\n\n    log('\\n=== API /api/ukb/status (first 2000 chars) ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(apiData, null, 2).substring(0, 2000));\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write('Error: ' + err.message + '\\n');\n    process.exit(1);\n  } finally {\n    await browser.close();\n  }\n})();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```

```

await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# Find where playwright is installed\nfind /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED> -path \"*/node_modules/playwright/index.js\" -maxdepth 6 2>/dev/null | head -3",
  "description": "Find playwright installation"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/node_modules/playwright/index.js
/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/.npm/_npx/9833c18b2d85bc59/node_modules/playwright/index.js
/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/.npm/_npx/e41f203b7505f1fb/node_modules/playwright/index.js
```


---

### Bash - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# Dashboard on 3032 might be the static frontend with API on 3033\ncurl -s http://localhost:3032 2>/dev/null | head -5\necho \"===\"\ncurl -s http://localhost:3033 2>/dev/null | head -5",
  "description": "Check dashboard ports"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> charset="UTF-8" />
    <link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/health-icon.svg" />
===
Found. Redirecting to http://localhost:3032
```

### Edit - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/tmp/pw-scripts/debug-wf-graph.js",
  "old_string": "    await page.goto('http://localhost:3032', { waitUntil: 'networkidle', timeout: 15000 });",
  "new_string": "    await page.goto('http://localhost:3032', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded', timeout: 15000 });\n    await page.waitForTimeout(3000); // Let React render"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
The file /tmp/pw-scripts/debug-wf-graph.js has been updated successfully.
```

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/pw-scripts/debug-substeps.js",
  "content": "const { chromium } = require('playwright');\n\n(async () => {\n  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });\n  const context = await browser.newContext({ viewport: { width: 1400, height: 900 } });\n  const page = await context.newPage();\n  const log = (msg) => process.stdout.write(msg + '\\n');\n\n  try {\n    await page.goto('http://localhost:3032', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded', timeout: 15000 });\n    await page.waitForTimeout(3000);\n\n    // Open UKB modal\n    await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');\n    await page.waitForTimeout(2000);\n\n    // Click on the Semantic node to see sub-steps\n    const semanticNode = await page.locator('[data-testid=\"workflow-node-semantic_analysis\"]');\n    if (await semanticNode.count() > 0) {\n      await semanticNode.click();\n      await page.waitForTimeout(1000);\n    }\n\n    // Screenshot after clicking semantic node\n    await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/wf-substeps.png', fullPage: false });\n\n    // Get the right panel content (sub-steps detail)\n    const rightPanel = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      // Find the detail panel - look for substep indicators\n      const panel = document.querySelector('[class*=\"detail\"], [class*=\"panel\"], [class*=\"sidebar\"]');\n      if (panel) {\n        return {\n          html: panel.innerHTML.substring(0, 3000),\n          text: panel.textContent?.substring(0, 1000)\n        };\n      }\n      return null;\n    });\n\n    log('=== RIGHT PANEL ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(rightPanel?.text, null, 2));\n\n    // Get workflow progress data from the API\n    const progressData = await page.evaluate(async () => {\n      try {\n        const resp = await fetch('/api/ukb/status');\n        const data = await resp.json();\n        // Focus on the current step details\n        const wf = data?.data || data;\n        return {\n          status: wf.status,\n          currentStep: wf.currentStep,\n          currentSubstep: wf.currentSubstep,\n          completedSteps: wf.completedSteps,\n          stepsDetail: wf.stepsDetail?.map(s => ({\n            name: s.name,\n            status: s.status,\n            substeps: s.substeps?.map(ss => ({ id: ss.id, status: ss.status, name: ss.name }))\n          }))\n        };\n      } catch (e) {\n        return { error: e.message };\n      }\n    });\n\n    log('\\n=== PROGRESS DATA ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(progressData, null, 2));\n\n    // Also check the raw progress file\n    const rawProgress = await page.evaluate(async () => {\n      try {\n        const resp = await fetch('/api/ukb/progress');\n        return await resp.json();\n      } catch (e) {\n        return { error: e.message };\n      }\n    });\n\n    log('\\n=== RAW PROGRESS (first 3000 chars) ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(rawProgress, null, 2).substring(0, 3000));\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write('Error: ' + err.message + '\\n');\n    process.exit(1);\n  } finally {\n    await browser.close();\n  }\n})();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/pw-scripts/debug-substeps.js
```

### Bash - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "NODE_PATH=/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/node_modules node /tmp/pw-scripts/debug-substeps.js 2>&1",
  "description": "Debug sub-step rendering",
  "timeout": 30000
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
=== RIGHT PANEL ===
undefined

=== PROGRESS DATA ===
{
  "error": "Unexpected token '<', \"<!doctype \"... is not valid JSON"
}

=== RAW PROGRESS (first 3000 chars) ===
{
  "error": "Unexpected token '<', \"<!doctype \"... is not valid JSON"
}
```

### Read - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>reshMiddleware.ts",
  "offset": 390,
  "limit": 60
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
   390→
   391→            // Log batch iteration details if available
   392→            if (p.batchIterations?.length > 0) {
   393→              const currentBatch = p.batchIterations[p.batchIterations.length - 1]
   394→              if (currentBatch) {
   395→                const runningSteps = currentBatch.steps?.filter((s: any) => s.status === 'running') || []
   396→                const completedSteps = currentBatch.steps?.filter((s: any) => s.status === 'completed') || []
   397→
   3
...[truncated]
```

  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/src/components/ukb-workflow-graph.tsx",
  "offset": 1550,
  "limit": 60
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
  1550→  const getNodeStatus = (agentId: string): 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'skipped' | 'paused' => {
  1551→    // Check if this agent's step is currently paused in single-step mode
  1552→    if (process.stepPaused && process.pausedAtStep) {
  1553→      // Map the pausedAtStep (workflow step name) to agent ID
  1554→      const pausedAgentId = STEP_TO_AGENT[process.pausedAtStep] || process.pausedAtStep
  1555→      if (pausedAgentId === agentId) {
  1556→        return 
...[truncated]
```

console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/src/components/ukb-workflow-graph.tsx",
  "offset": 1425,
  "limit": 80
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
  1425→          // Non-batch steps (pre-batch and finalization): use aggregate status
  1426→          // If multiple steps map to same agent, prefer the latest status
  1427→          // Create a shallow copy to avoid mutating Redux state
  1428→          if (!map[agentId] || step.status === 'running' || (step.status === 'completed' && map[agentId].status !== 'running')) {
  1429→            map[agentId] = { ...step }
  1430→          }
  1431→        }
  1432→
  1433→        // NOTE: stepToAg
...[truncated]
```

### Read - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```
