}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# Check the current workflow progress to see what currentStep looks like\npython3 -c \"\nimport json\nd = json.load(open('.data/workflow-progress.json'))\nprint('currentStep:', d.get('currentStep'))\nprint('currentSubstep:', d.get('currentSubstep'))\nprint('completedSteps:', d.get('completedSteps'))\nprint('status:', d.get('status'))\nsteps = d.get('steps', [])\nfor s in steps:\n    print(f'  step: {s.get(\\\"name\\\")} status={s.get(\\\"status\\\")}')\n\"",
  "description": "Check workflow progress data"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
currentStep: None
currentSubstep: None
completedSteps: None
status: running
```


---

### Bash - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash

   node -e "

   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# Check the full progress structure\npython3 -c \"\nimport json\nd = json.load(open('.data/workflow-progress.json'))\n# Show all keys\nfor k in sorted(d.keys()):\n    v = d[k]\n    if isinstance(v, (str, int, float, bool, type(None))):\n        print(f'{k}: {v}')\n    elif isinstance(v, list):\n        print(f'{k}: [{len(v)} items]')\n    elif isinstance(v, dict):\n        print(f'{k}: {{{len(v)} keys}}')\n\" 2>/dev/null",
  "description": "Check progress structure"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
config: {4 keys}
llmState: {3 keys}
mockLLM: True
mockLLMDelay: 500
pausedAt: 2026-03-14T14:46:51.215Z
pausedAtStep: sem_observation_gen
progress: {9 keys}
singleStepMode: True
status: running
stepIntoSubsteps: True
stepPaused: True
subStatus: executing-step
workflowId: wf-1773499589472
workflowName: wave-analysis
```

| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Grep
**Input:** ```json
{
  "pattern": "currentStep|currentSubstep|completedSteps|pausedAtStep",
  "path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/src/store/slices/ukbSlice.ts",
  "output_mode": "content",
  "-n": true,
  "head_limit": 20
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```

### Read - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/src/store/slices/ukbSlice.ts",
  "offset": 195,
  "limit": 80
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
   195→  pid: number | string  // Can be 'mcp-inline' for inline MCP workflows
   196→  workflowName: string
   197→  team: string
   198→  repositoryPath: string
   199→  startTime: string
   200→  lastHeartbeat: string
   201→  status: string
   202→  completedSteps: number
   203→  totalSteps: number
   204→  batchPhaseStepCount?: number  // Derived from workflow YAML (replaces hardcoded BATCH_STEP_COUNT)
   205→  currentStep: string | null
   206→  logFile: string | null
   207→  isAlive: bo
...[truncated]
```

fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/server.js",
  "offset": 650,
  "limit": 80
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
   650→                const lastUpdate = new Date(workflowProgress.lastUpdate).getTime();
   651→                const age = Date.now() - lastUpdate;
   652→                const hasFailed = (workflowProgress.stepsFailed?.length || 0) > 0;
   653→
   654→                // Check if this workflow is already represented in registered processes
   655→                // Only consider ALIVE processes - dead/failed ones should not block detection
   656→                const alreadyRegistered = deta
...[truncated]
```

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

})();

cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/server.js",
  "offset": 1050,
  "limit": 50
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
  1050→                    name: waveName,
  1051→                    status,
  1052→                    startTime: status !== 'pending' ? progress.startTime : null,
  1053→                };
  1054→            });
  1055→        }
  1056→
  1057→        return {
  1058→            status: state.status === 'paused' ? 'running' : state.status,
  1059→            workflowName: state.workflowName || 'wave-analysis',
  1060→            team: 'coding',
  1061→            startTime: progress.startTime
...[truncated]
```

### Read - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/server.js",
  "offset": 793,
  "limit": 10
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
   793→                    if (proc.status === 'running' && workflowProgress.workflowName === proc.workflowName) {
   794→                        proc.completedSteps = workflowProgress.completedSteps || 0;
   795→                        proc.totalSteps = workflowProgress.totalSteps || 0;
   796→                        proc.currentStep = workflowProgress.currentStep;
   797→                        proc.stepsCompleted = workflowProgress.stepsCompleted || [];
   798→                        proc.ste
...[truncated]
```

### Edit - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`

   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |

| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |

## 6. Output

- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/server.js",
  "old_string": "                        proc.completedSteps = workflowProgress.completedSteps || 0;\n                        proc.totalSteps = workflowProgress.totalSteps || 0;\n                        proc.currentStep = workflowProgress.currentStep;\n                        proc.stepsCompleted = workflowProgress.stepsCompleted || [];\n                        proc.stepsFailed = workflowProgress.stepsFailed || [];\n                        proc.elapsedSeconds = workflowProgress.elapsedSeconds || 0;",
  "new_string": "                        proc.completedSteps = workflowProgress.completedSteps || 0;\n                        proc.totalSteps = workflowProgress.totalSteps || 0;\n                        proc.currentStep = workflowProgress.currentStep || workflowProgress.progress?.currentSubstepId || workflowProgress.progress?.currentStepName || null;\n                        proc.stepsCompleted = workflowProgress.stepsCompleted || workflowProgress.progress?.completedSteps || [];\n                        proc.stepsFailed = workflowProgress.stepsFailed || [];\n                        proc.elapsedSeconds = workflowProgress.elapsedSeconds || workflowProgress.progress?.elapsedSeconds || 0;"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
The file <AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/server.js has been updated successfully.
```

  "file_path": "/tmp/pw-scripts/verify-substeps.js",
  "content": "const { chromium } = require('playwright');\n\n(async () => {\n  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });\n  const context = await browser.newContext({ viewport: { width: 1400, height: 900 } });\n  const page = await context.newPage();\n  const log = (msg) => process.stdout.write(msg + '\\n');\n\n  try {\n    await page.goto('http://localhost:3032', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded', timeout: 15000 });\n    await page.waitForTimeout(3000);\n\n    // Open UKB modal\n    await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');\n    await page.waitForTimeout(3000);\n\n    // Get all workflow nodes with their statuses\n    const nodes = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid^=\"workflow-node-\"]')).map(node => ({\n        id: node.getAttribute('data-testid'),\n        status: node.getAttribute('data-status'),\n      }));\n    });\n\n    log('=== NODE STATUSES ===');\n    for (const n of nodes) {\n      const icon = n.status === 'completed' ? '✅' : n.status === 'running' ? '🔵' : n.status === 'paused' ? '⏸️' : '⬜';\n      log(`  ${icon} ${n.id}: ${n.status}`);\n    }\n\n    // Get all sub-step elements and their statuses\n    const substeps = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid^=\"substep-\"]')).map(el => ({\n        id: el.getAttribute('data-testid'),\n        status: el.getAttribute('data-status'),\n      }));\n    });\n\n    log('\\n=== SUB-STEP STATUSES ===');\n    for (const s of substeps) {\n      const icon = s.status === 'completed' ? '✅' : s.status === 'running' ? '🔵' : s.status === 'paused' ? '⏸️' : '⬜';\n      log(`  ${icon} ${s.id}: ${s.status}`);\n    }\n\n    // Screenshot\n    await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/wf-after-fix.png', fullPage: false });\n    log('\\nScreenshot: /tmp/pw-scripts/wf-after-fix.png');\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write('Error: ' + err.message + '\\n');\n    process.exit(1);\n  } finally {\n    await browser.close();\n  }\n})();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/pw-scripts/verify-substeps.js
```

### Bash - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "NODE_PATH=/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/node_modules node /tmp/pw-scripts/verify-substeps.js 2>&1",
  "description": "Verify sub-step statuses after fix",
  "timeout": 30000
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
=== NODE STATUSES ===
  🔵 workflow-node-orchestrator: running
  ✅ workflow-node-batch_scheduler: completed
  ⬜ workflow-node-kg_operators: inactive
  ⬜ workflow-node-batch_checkpoint_manager: inactive
  ⬜ workflow-node-git_history: inactive
  ⬜ workflow-node-vibe_history: inactive
  ⬜ workflow-node-code_graph: inactive
  ⬜ workflow-node-documentation_linker: inactive
  🔵 workflow-node-semantic_analysis: running
  ⬜ workflow-node-web_search: inactive
  ⬜ workflow-node-insight_generation: inacti
...[truncated]
```

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/pw-scripts/expand-substeps.js",
  "content": "const { chromium } = require('playwright');\n\n(async () => {\n  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });\n  const context = await browser.newContext({ viewport: { width: 1400, height: 900 } });\n  const page = await context.newPage();\n  const log = (msg) => process.stdout.write(msg + '\\n');\n\n  try {\n    await page.goto('http://localhost:3032', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded', timeout: 15000 });\n    await page.waitForTimeout(3000);\n\n    // Open UKB modal\n    await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');\n    await page.waitForTimeout(2000);\n\n    // Click on Semantic node to expand sub-steps\n    const semanticNode = page.locator('[data-testid=\"workflow-node-semantic_analysis\"]');\n    await semanticNode.click();\n    await page.waitForTimeout(2000);\n\n    // Screenshot after clicking\n    await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/wf-semantic-expanded.png', fullPage: false });\n\n    // Check for sub-step elements now\n    const substeps = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid^=\"substep-\"]')).map(el => ({\n        id: el.getAttribute('data-testid'),\n        status: el.getAttribute('data-status'),\n      }));\n    });\n\n    log('=== SUB-STEPS AFTER CLICK ===');\n    if (substeps.length === 0) {\n      log('  No sub-step elements found');\n\n      // Check if the right panel shows sub-step info\n      const rightPanelText = await page.evaluate(() => {\n        // Look for the detail sidebar\n        const panels = document.querySelectorAll('[class*=\"panel\"], [class*=\"sidebar\"], [class*=\"detail\"]');\n        for (const p of panels) {\n          if (p.textContent?.includes('Sub-step') || p.textContent?.includes('substep') || p.textContent?.includes('Processing')) {\n            return p.textContent?.substring(0, 500);\n          }\n        }\n        // Fallback: get all text from the modal\n        const modal = document.querySelector('[role=\"dialog\"], [class*=\"modal\"]');\n        if (modal) return modal.textContent?.substring(modal.textContent.length - 500);\n        return null;\n      });\n      log('  Right panel text: ' + (rightPanelText?.substring(0, 300) || 'none'));\n    } else {\n      for (const s of substeps) {\n        const icon = s.status === 'completed' ? '✅' : s.status === 'running' ? '🔵' : '⬜';\n        log(`  ${icon} ${s.id}: ${s.status}`);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Check: what does the API return for currentStep now?\n    const apiResp = await page.evaluate(async () => {\n      try {\n        const resp = await fetch('http://localhost:3033/api/ukb/status');\n        const data = await resp.json();\n        const proc = data?.data?.processes?.[0];\n        return {\n          currentStep: proc?.currentStep,\n          pausedAtStep: proc?.pausedAtStep,\n          completedSteps: proc?.completedSteps,\n          stepsCount: proc?.steps?.length,\n          stepNames: proc?.steps?.map(s => `${s.name}:${s.status}`).slice(0, 10)\n        };\n      } catch (e) {\n        return { error: e.message };\n      }\n    });\n\n    log('\\n=== API DATA ===');\n    log(JSON.stringify(apiResp, null, 2));\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write('Error: ' + err.message + '\\n');\n    process.exit(1);\n  } finally {\n    await browser.close();\n  }\n})();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/pw-scripts/expand-substeps.js
```

  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "NODE_PATH=/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/node_modules node /tmp/pw-scripts/expand-substeps.js 2>&1",
  "description": "Expand and check sub-steps",
  "timeout": 30000
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
=== SUB-STEPS AFTER CLICK ===
  No sub-step elements found
  Right panel text: Enrichment: Enrich entities with additional context and metadata (Pending)EnrSemantic AnalysisPendingDeep code analysis to detect patterns (MVC, Factory, Observer, etc.), assess <USER_ID_REDACTED> metrics, identify anti-patterns, and generate LLM-powered insights on architecture.TechnologyLLMGroq: llama-3.3-70

=== API DATA ===
{}
```


---

### Bash - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`

   ```bash

     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# The API returned empty {}. Let me check directly:\ncurl -s http://localhost:3033/api/ukb/status 2>/dev/null | python3 -c \"\nimport sys,json\nd = json.load(sys.stdin)\nprocs = d.get('data', {}).get('processes', [])\nif procs:\n    p = procs[0]\n    print('currentStep:', p.get('currentStep'))\n    print('pausedAtStep:', p.get('pausedAtStep'))\n    print('completedSteps:', p.get('completedSteps'))\n    print('steps count:', len(p.get('steps', [])))\n    for s in (p.get('steps') or [])[:5]:\n        print(f'  {s.get(\\\"name\\\")}: {s.get(\\\"status\\\")}')\nelse:\n    print('No processes')\n    print('Keys:', list(d.get('data', {}).keys()))\n\" 2>/dev/null",
  "description": "Check API directly"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
No processes
Keys: ['running', 'stale', 'frozen', 'total', 'timestamp']
```

| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# WF is still running but API returns 0 processes. The server.js probably\n# crashed after our edit. Check Docker:\ndocker exec coding-services supervisorctl status web-services:health-dashboard 2>/dev/null",
  "description": "Check dashboard server status"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
web-services:health-dashboard    RUNNING   pid 10091, uptime 0:02:03
```

### Bash - 2026-03-14 14:47:53 UTC [15:47:53 CEST]

**User Request:** # Playwright CLI Skill

Drive a real Chromium browser from the bash_tool using Playwright (Node.js). No MCP server needed.

---

## 1. Environment Setup

Always run this check first. It's fast and idempotent.

```bash
# Check Node + npx availability
node --version && npx --version

# Check if playwright is available; install if not
if ! npx playwright --version 2>/dev/null; then
  echo "Installing Playwright..."
  npm install -D playwright 2>&1 | tail -5
  npx playwright install chromium 2>&1 | tail -10
fi
```

If `npm install` fails due to network restrictions, inform the user that Playwright must be pre-installed in their environment.

**Working directory:** Write scripts to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and run from there. For E2E test specs, use the project's `tests/e2e/` directory structure.

---

## 2. Script Patterns

Write a Node.js script, save it, run it with `node`. Always use these boilerplate patterns:

### Boilerplate (all scripts)

```js
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  try {
    // --- your task here ---
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
  }
})();
```

### Screenshot

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.screenshot({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/screenshot.png', fullPage: true });
console.log('Screenshot saved.');
```

### PDF

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
await page.pdf({ path: '/tmp/pw-scripts/output.pdf', format: 'A4' });
console.log('PDF saved.');
```

### Web Scraping

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });

// Wait for a key element if needed
await page.waitForSelector('.content', { timeout: 10000 });

const data = await page.evaluate(() => {
  // Run in browser context — return serialisable data
  return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('h2')).map(el => el.textContent.trim());
});

console.log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
```

### Form Fill & Click

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com/login');
await page.fill('#username', 'myuser');
await page.fill('#password', 'mypass');
await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
await page.waitForNavigation({ waitUntil: 'networkidle' });
console.log('Current URL:', page.url());
```

### UI Test (assertion-style)

```js
await page.goto('https://example.com');
const title = await page.title();
console.assert(title.includes('Example'), `Unexpected title: ${title}`);

const btn = await page.$('button.cta');
console.assert(btn !== null, 'CTA button not found');
console.log('PASS');
```

### E2E Test with Playwright Test Runner

For structured E2E tests, use the Playwright test runner:

```bash
# Run all E2E tests in a directory
cd tests/e2e/dashboard && npx playwright test --reporter=line

# Run a specific test file
npx playwright test workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts --reporter=line

# Run tests matching a pattern
npx playwright test -g "green nodes" --reporter=line

# Run with visible browser (debug)
npx playwright test --headed --reporter=line

# View test trace on failure
npx playwright show-trace test-results/*/trace.zip
```

---

## 3. Dashboard-Specific Patterns

For testing the System Health Dashboard (localhost:3032):

### Navigate to UKB Workflow Modal

```js
await page.goto('http://localhost:3032');
// Click the "UKB Workflows" card to open the modal
await page.click('text=UKB Workflows');
// Wait for graph nodes to render
await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^="workflow-node-"]', { timeout: 15000 });
```

### Check Node Status (green/running/pending)

```js
const node = await page.locator('[data-testid="workflow-node-semantic_analysis"]');
const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status');
console.log(`semantic_analysis status: ${status}`);
// Expected: 'completed' (green), 'running' (blue), 'pending' (gray)
```

### Inject Workflow Progress (for testing)

```js
const fs = require('fs');
const progressPath = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';
fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify({
  workflowId: 'wf_test',
  workflowName: 'wave-analysis',
  status: 'running',
  progress: {
    completedSteps: ['wave1'],
    currentWave: 2,
    totalWaves: 4,
    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',
    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',
    startTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),
  },
  config: { singleStepMode: true, mockLLM: true },
  stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],
}, null, 2));
```

---

## 4. Workflow

1. **Understand the task** — URL, goal, any credentials or selectors needed.
2. **Setup** — Run the environment check (Section 1).
3. **Write script** — Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js` using Write tool or heredoc.
4. **Run** — `node /tmp/pw-scripts/pw_task.js`
5. **Handle output** — If screenshots/PDFs produced, tell user the file path.
6. **Iterate** — If selectors fail, inspect the page HTML first:
   ```bash
   # Quick DOM dump for debugging
   node -e "
   const {chromium} = require('playwright');
   (async()=>{
     const b = await chromium.launch({headless:true});
     const p = await b.newPage();
     await p.goto('URL_HERE', {waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'});
     console.log(await p.content());
     await b.close();
   })();" 2>/dev/null | head -200
   ```

---

## 5. Tips & Gotchas

| Situation | Solution |
|---|---|
| Page content loads late (JS-rendered) | Use `waitUntil: 'networkidle'` or `page.waitForSelector()` |
| Need to extract structured data | Use `page.evaluate()` — runs in browser context |
| Need to capture network responses | Use `page.on('response', ...)` before `goto` |
| Anti-bot / CAPTCHA | Inform user — automation cannot reliably bypass these |
| Large pages for PDF | Add `printBackground: true` to pdf options |
| File downloads | Set `context = browser.newContext({ acceptDownloads: true })` |
| Auth via cookies/session | Use `context.addCookies([...])` before navigation |
| Screenshots of specific element | `const el = await page.$('.selector'); await el.screenshot({path: '...'})` |
| Dashboard not responding | Check `curl -s http://localhost:3032` first, rebuild if needed |

---

## 6. Output

- **Screenshots/PDFs:** Save to `/tmp/pw-scripts/` and tell user the path.
- **Scraped data:** Print to stdout (JSON preferred), then summarise key findings for the user.
- **Test results:** Print PASS/FAIL per assertion, summarise at end.
- **Errors:** Always include the URL, the failing selector or step, and the raw error message.

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# Server is running but returning no processes. Let me check server stderr for errors:\ndocker exec coding-services supervisorctl tail -100 web-services:health-dashboard stderr 2>/dev/null | tail -20",
  "description": "Check server error logs"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
web-services:health-dashboard: ERROR (unknown error reading log)
```

{
  "command": "# Check the last update on the progress file - the server may see it as stale\npython3 -c \"\nimport json, time\nd = json.load(open('.data/workflow-progress.json'))\np = d.get('progress', {})\nlast = p.get('lastUpdate')\nprint('lastUpdate:', last)\nif last:\n    from datetime import datetime\n    ts = datetime.fromisoformat(last.replace('Z', '+00:00')).timestamp()\n    age = time.time() - ts\n    print(f'age: {age:.0f}s ({age/60:.1f}min)')\n\"",

}

lastUpdate: 2026-03-14T14:46:51.153Z
age: 746s (12.4min)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "# 12 minutes stale! The WF is paused at a step but the progress hasn't been updated.\n# The server considers it stale (>5 min) and then checks if totalSteps == 0 → race condition\n# Let me refresh the lastUpdate timestamp to make it fresh:\npython3 -c \"\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\nd = json.load(open('.data/workflow-progress.json'))\nd['progress']['lastUpdate'] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat().replace('+00:00', 'Z')\njson.dump(d, open('.data/workflow-progress.json', 'w'), indent=2)\nprint('Updated lastUpdate')\n\"\n# Now check the API again:\nsleep 2\ncurl -s http://localhost:3033/api/ukb/status 2>/dev/null | python3 -c \"\nimport sys,json\nd = json.load(sys.stdin)\nprocs = d.get('data', {}).get('processes', [])\nprint(f'{len(procs)} processes')\nif procs:\n    p = procs[0]\n    print('currentStep:', p.get('currentStep'))\n    print('pausedAtStep:', p.get('pausedAtStep'))\n\"",
  "description": "Refresh progress timestamp and check API"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
Updated lastUpdate
0 processes
```
